[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The LZW decompression code in `[0m[1;35mLZWInputStream.initializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaxCodeSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` allocates two arrays [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`prefixes` and `characters`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m of size `[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m << [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaxCodeSize` without any upper bound, and the default Z-compressor harness passes a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheader‐derived `maxCodeSize` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m plus a `memoryLimitInKiB` of [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m, which bypasses[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe limit check.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A malicious or corrupt `.Z` header can set `maxCodeSize` near the type width [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mup to [0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, causing huge array allocations and a Java heap space OutOfMemoryError.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Functionality[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Legitimate `.Z` streams use a small default code size [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtypically [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m bits, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgrowing to [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m bits in LZW[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; existing valid data must continue to decompress.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must not alter the fuzzer harness or tests; only source logic in the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompressor classes.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We should avoid too‐broad catches or removal of functionality. We introduce a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhard cap on `maxCodeSize`, plus honoring an optional memory limit if configured.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Outline[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Introduce a sensible hard cap on `maxCodeSize` in `ZCompressorInputStream` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprior to any table allocation:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Define a new constant, e.g. `MAX_REASONABLE_CODE_SIZE = [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmatching classic LZW max code size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. After extracting `maxCodeSize` from the header byte, validate:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize < [0m[1;35mgetInitialCodeSize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || maxCodeSize > [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMAX_REASONABLE_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                throw new [0m[1;35mCompressorException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Invalid LZW maxCodeSize "[0m[39m + [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaxCodeSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. This prevents `[0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` from ever receiving values above the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcap.[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Harden `[0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint maxCodeSize, int memoryLimitInKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Even when `memoryLimitInKiB < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`, treat it as “no custom limit” but still [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menforce a library‐wide safe maximum table size via the same [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MAX_REASONABLE_CODE_SIZE`.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. At the start of this method, compute `int cap = [0m[1;35mMath.min[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMAX_REASONABLE_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` and proceed with `cap` for allocation.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Align both overloads:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Redirect the single‐argument version to call the two‐argument version with[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`memoryLimitInKiB` = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, so the safe maximum check always applies.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Remove/adjust the existing check that throws on `[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m << maxCodeSize < [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor `[0m[1;35mgetCodeSize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m > maxCodeSize` to apply after bounding.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Step-by-Step Implementation[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. In `ZCompressorInputStream` constructor [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m81[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m88[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Right after `maxCodeSize = thirdByte & MAX_CODE_SIZE_MASK;`[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Insert:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          final int HARD_CAP = [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m; [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m or extract to class constant[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize < DEFAULT_CODE_SIZE || maxCodeSize > HARD_CAP[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              throw new [0m[1;35mCompressorException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"LZW maxCodeSize "[0m[39m + maxCodeSize + [0m[32m" [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mout of permitted range [0m[32m[[0m[32m"[0m[39m [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                                            + DEFAULT_CODE_SIZE + [0m[32m","[0m[39m + HARD_CAP + [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"[0m[32m][0m[32m"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. In `LZWInputStream`:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Declare a new private static constant:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          private static final int MAX_REASONABLE_CODE_SIZE = [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Modify `[0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint maxCodeSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to:[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          protected void [0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint maxCodeSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize, [0m[35m/[0m[39m* library default limit *[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – At the top of `[0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint maxCodeSize, int memoryLimitInKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Validate against the new cap:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             ```[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize > MAX_REASONABLE_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 throw new [0m[1;35mIllegalArgumentException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"maxCodeSize "[0m[39m [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                     + maxCodeSize + [0m[32m" exceeds hard cap of "[0m[39m + [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMAX_REASONABLE_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             ```[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Compute `maxTableSize = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m << maxCodeSize;` and, if `memoryLimitInKiB [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m>= [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`, ensure `maxTableSize * entryOverhead` doesn't exceed it. If [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`memoryLimitInKiB < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`, skip custom limit but rely on the hard cap.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Ensure existing sanity checks [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m << maxCodeSize < [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mgetCodeSize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m> maxCodeSize`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m run *after* this cap enforcement.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Introducing a hard cap prevents any header from requesting unreasonable table [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msizes, eliminating the OOM condition on malicious inputs.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Valid `.Z` archives never require code sizes above [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m bits; capping at [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m bits[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis a conservative safety margin.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By centralizing the cap in `LZWInputStream`, other entry points [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif any[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbenefit from the same protection.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The two‐argument overload still supports a user‐configured memory limit; [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpassing `[0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m` now means “use default cap,” not unbounded.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Side Effects and Mitigations[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If valid streams ever use code sizes above the cap, they will now be rejected.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWe choose a cap above the historic maximum [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m12[0m[39m bits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to avoid false positives.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing tests for compression/decompression should be run; any failures would[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicate the cap is too low. Adjust the constant accordingly.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness or test code changes are required; tests that invoke `Expander` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill see `CompressorException` instead of OOM on malicious data.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. References & Consistency[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar hard‐cap patterns exist in other decompressors [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `Pack200`, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Zip`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, where header‐derived sizes are validated against library constants.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This fix aligns `ZCompressorInputStream` and `LZWInputStream` with the general[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCommons Compress policy of “safe defaults” plus optional explicit limits.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/lzw/LZWInputStrea[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mm.java: top [0m[1;39m([0m[39mconstant declaration[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/lzw/LZWInputStrea[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mm.java: initializeTables methods<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/z/ZCompressorInpu[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtStream.java: constructor<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- During a Jazzer-driven fuzzing session, the input to `ExpanderFuzzer` caused [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.compress.compressors.lzw.LZWInputStream.initializeTables` to [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This led to `java.lang.OutOfMemoryError: Java heap space`, surfaced as a [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueLow: Out of memory`.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The stack trace pinpoints initialization logic in [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mLZWInputStream.initializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint maxCodeSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, triggered via [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ZCompressorInputStream` and propagating up to the expander example.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImportant observations  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The log shows instrumentation of many classes before the crash but the root [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfailure is the unbounded allocation in LZW’s table initialization.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The OOM occurs before any explicit memory checks or limits in LZWInputStream, so [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe code attempts to allocate arrays sized `[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m << maxCodeSize` without verifying [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreasonability.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Revert the malformed last patch entirely so that `LZWInputStream.java` returns [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto the initial code structure [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrestoring the original single- and two-argument [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`initializeTables` methods and their braces[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. This ensures we start from a clean, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompilable baseline.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Introduce a new constant to cap the code size:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `LZWInputStream.java`, immediately after the existing `DEFAULT_CODE_SIZE` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeclaration, add:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       * Upper bound to prevent unbounded dictionary allocations [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m << [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaxCodeSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      protected static final int MAX_REASONABLE_CODE_SIZE = [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. This constant keeps the allowable `maxCodeSize` within a safe range [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m<<[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m = [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m [0m[1;36m536[0m[39m entries[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Augment the single-argument `[0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint maxCodeSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to enforce the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mupper bound:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. At the very start of the method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbefore any bit‐shifts[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, insert:[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize > MAX_REASONABLE_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          throw new [0m[1;35mIllegalArgumentException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"maxCodeSize "[0m[39m + maxCodeSize[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              + [0m[32m" exceeds allowed maximum of "[0m[39m + MAX_REASONABLE_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Leave the rest of the method intact [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe existing lower-bound check for `[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m <<[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaxCodeSize < [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m` and initialization loop[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, preserving its logic and braces.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Similarly, guard the two-argument `[0m[1;35minitializeTables[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint maxCodeSize, int [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemoryLimitInKiB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Immediately after the existing check for `maxCodeSize <= [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`, add:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCodeSize > MAX_REASONABLE_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          throw new [0m[1;35mIllegalArgumentException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"maxCodeSize "[0m[39m + maxCodeSize[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              + [0m[32m" exceeds allowed maximum of "[0m[39m + MAX_REASONABLE_CODE_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Keep its memory‐limit check and subsequent delegation to the single-argument [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod unchanged.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. No other modifications:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not alter the harness or fuzzing logic.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not remove or replace any functionality beyond adding these preconditions.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure method signatures, throws clauses, and braces remain properly balanced.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mExplanation and Justification:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- By capping `maxCodeSize` to [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m, we limit array allocations to at most [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m<<[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentries [0m[1;39m([0m[39m~[0m[1;36m65[0m[39m [0m[1;36m536[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, preventing heap exhaustion from maliciously large inputs.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Inserting the bounds checks at the very start of each `initializeTables` overload[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavoids disturbing existing code blocks or loops, and retains the original exception[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msemantics for too‐small values.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Keeping both overloads ensures that callers [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `ZCompressorInputStream`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstill resolve to the appropriate method without signature mismatches.[0m               [2m                [0m
